SELECT [h0].[Id], [h0].[Accion], [h0].[Fecha], [h0].[Ip], [h0].[UsuarioId], [d].[Id], [d].[Cantidad], [d].[Descripcion], [d].[HistorialProductoId], [d].[NombreProducto], [d].[Precio]
FROM (
    SELECT [h].[Id], [h].[Accion], [h].[Fecha], [h].[Ip], [h].[UsuarioId]
    FROM [HistorialProductos] AS [h]
    ORDER BY (SELECT 1)
    OFFSET @__p_0 ROWS FETCH NEXT @__p_1 ROWS ONLY
) AS [h0]
LEFT JOIN [DetalleHistorialProductos] AS [d] ON [h0].[Id] = [d].[HistorialProductoId]
ORDER BY [h0].[Id]
